// src/api/tasks.ts
import { apiFetch } from './client';

export type TimeReward = 'NONE' | 'MIN_15' | 'HOUR_1' | 'NEG_MIN_15' | 'NEG_HOUR_1';

export type Task = {
  code: string;
  name: string;
  category: string;
  time_reward: TimeReward;
  money_reward_eur: string | number; // n8n can return string or number
};

export async function getTasks() {
  return apiFetch<Task[]>('/api/tasks', { method: 'GET' });
}
2) Replace app/(tabs)/form.tsx with this
// app/(tabs)/form.tsx
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import {
  ActivityIndicator,
  SafeAreaView,
  ScrollView,
  Text,
  View,
} from 'react-native';
import { getTasks, Task, TimeReward } from '../../src/api/tasks';

function formatTime(t: TimeReward) {
  switch (t) {
    case 'MIN_15':
      return '15 min';
    case 'HOUR_1':
      return '1 hour';
    case 'NEG_MIN_15':
      return 'âˆ’15 min';
    case 'NEG_HOUR_1':
      return 'âˆ’1 hour';
    default:
      return 'â€“';
  }
}

function formatMoney(v: string | number) {
  const n = Number(v || 0);
  const sign = n < 0 ? '-' : '';
  return `${sign}â‚¬${Math.abs(n).toFixed(2)}`;
}

export default function FormScreen() {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<Task[]>([]);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Load tasks once on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    (async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true);
        setError(null);
        const data = await getTasks();
        if (!cancelled) setTasks(Array.isArray(data) ? data : []);
      } catch (e: any) {
        if (!cancelled) setError(e?.message || 'Failed to load tasks');
      } finally {
        if (!cancelled) setLoading(false);
      }
    })();
    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
    };
  }, []);

  // Group by category for display
  const groups = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<string, Task[]>();
    for (const t of tasks) {
      const k = t.category || 'Other';
      if (!map.has(k)) map.set(k, []);
      map.get(k)!.push(t);
    }
    // Sort categories and tasks by name for a stable UI
    const arr = Array.from(map.entries()).map(([category, items]) => ({
      category,
      items: items.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name)),
    }));
    return arr.sort((a, b) => a.category.localeCompare(b.category));
  }, [tasks]);

  return (
    <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }}>
      <ScrollView
        contentContainerStyle={{ padding: 24, gap: 16 }}
        keyboardShouldPersistTaps="handled"
      >
        <Text style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: '700', color: '#111' }}>
          Form
        </Text>

        {/* Loading */}
        {loading && (
          <View style={{ paddingVertical: 32, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            <ActivityIndicator />
            <Text style={{ marginTop: 8, color: '#666' }}>Loading tasksâ€¦</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Error */}
        {!loading && error && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fde7e9',
              borderColor: '#f2b2b8',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{error}</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Empty */}
        {!loading && !error && groups.length === 0 && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
              borderColor: '#eee',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 16,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#333', fontWeight: '600' }}>No tasks</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>
              There are no active tasks right now.
            </Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* List (read-only for step 2) */}
        {!loading &&
          !error &&
          groups.map(({ category, items }) => (
            <View
              key={category}
              style={{
                backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
                borderWidth: 1,
                borderColor: '#eee',
                borderRadius: 12,
                padding: 12,
                gap: 8,
              }}
            >
              <Text style={{ color: '#222', fontWeight: '700' }}>
                {category}
              </Text>

              {items.map((t) => (
                <View
                  key={t.code}
                  style={{
                    backgroundColor: '#fff',
                    borderWidth: 1,
                    borderColor: '#eee',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    padding: 12,
                    flexDirection: 'row',
                    justifyContent: 'space-between',
                    alignItems: 'center',
                  }}
                >
                  <View style={{ maxWidth: '60%' }}>
                    <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontWeight: '600' }}>
                      {t.name}
                    </Text>
                    <Text style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: 12 }}>
                      {formatTime(t.time_reward)} Â· {formatMoney(t.money_reward_eur)}
                    </Text>
                  </View>

                  {/* Quantity controls land here in Step 3 */}
                  <View
                    style={{
                      paddingVertical: 6,
                      paddingHorizontal: 10,
                      borderRadius: 999,
                      borderWidth: 1,
                      borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
                      backgroundColor: '#f8fafc',
                    }}
                  >
                    <Text style={{ color: '#999' }}>qty 0</Text>
                  </View>
                </View>
              ))}
            </View>
          ))}
      </ScrollView>
    </SafeAreaView>
  );
}

  switch (t) {
    case 'MIN_15':
      return '15 min';
    case 'HOUR_1':
      return '1 hour';
    case 'NEG_MIN_15':
      return 'âˆ’15 min';
    case 'NEG_HOUR_1':
      return 'âˆ’1 hour';
    default:
      return 'â€“';
  }

  const sign = n < 0 ? '-' : '';
  return `${sign}â‚¬${Math.abs(n).toFixed(2)}`;

type QtyMap = Record<string, number>;

export default function FormScreen() {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<Task[]>([]);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [qtys, setQtys] = useState<QtyMap>({}); // local quantities per task_code

  // Load tasks once on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    (async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true);
        setError(null);
        const data = await getTasks();
        const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
        if (!cancelled) {
          setTasks(arr);
          // initialize missing qtys to 0 (preserve existing)
          setQtys((prev) => {
            const next: QtyMap = { ...prev };
            for (const t of arr) if (next[t.code] == null) next[t.code] = 0;
            return next;
          });
        }
      } catch (e: any) {
        if (!cancelled) setError(e?.message || 'Failed to load tasks');
      } finally {
        if (!cancelled) setLoading(false);
      }
    })();
    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
    };
  }, []);

  // Group by category for display
  const groups = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<string, Task[]>();
    for (const t of tasks) {
      const k = t.category || 'Other';
      if (!map.has(k)) map.set(k, []);
      map.get(k)!.push(t);
    }
    // Sort categories and tasks by name for a stable UI
    const arr = Array.from(map.entries()).map(([category, items]) => ({
      category,
      items: items.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name)),
    }));
    return arr.sort((a, b) => a.category.localeCompare(b.category));
  }, [tasks]);

  // Helpers to mutate qtys safely
  const clamp = (n: number) => Math.max(0, Math.min(999, Number.isFinite(n) ? Math.trunc(n) : 0));
  const setQty = (code: string, value: number) =>
    setQtys((prev) => ({ ...prev, [code]: clamp(value) }));
  const inc = (code: string) => setQty(code, (qtys[code] || 0) + 1);
  const dec = (code: string) => setQty(code, (qtys[code] || 0) - 1);
  const onEdit = (code: string, text: string) => {
    const digitsOnly = text.replace(/[^\d]/g, '');
    setQty(code, digitsOnly === '' ? 0 : parseInt(digitsOnly, 10));
  };

  const totalSelected = useMemo(
    () => Object.values(qtys).reduce((a, b) => a + (Number.isFinite(b) ? b : 0), 0),
    [qtys]
  );

  return (
    <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }}>
      <ScrollView
        contentContainerStyle={{ padding: 24, gap: 16 }}
        keyboardShouldPersistTaps="handled"
      >
        <Text style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: '700', color: '#111' }}>
          Form
        </Text>

        {/* Loading */}
        {loading && (
          <View style={{ paddingVertical: 32, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            <ActivityIndicator />
            <Text style={{ marginTop: 8, color: '#666' }}>Loading tasksâ€¦</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Error */}
        {!loading && error && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fde7e9',
              borderColor: '#f2b2b8',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{error}</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Empty */}
        {!loading && !error && groups.length === 0 && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
              borderColor: '#eee',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 16,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#333', fontWeight: '600' }}>No tasks</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>
              There are no active tasks right now.
            </Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* List with quantity controls */}
        {!loading &&
          !error &&
          groups.map(({ category, items }) => (
            <View
              key={category}
              style={{
                backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
                borderWidth: 1,
                borderColor: '#eee',
                borderRadius: 12,
                padding: 12,
                gap: 8,
              }}
            >
              <Text style={{ color: '#222', fontWeight: '700' }}>
                {category}
              </Text>

              {items.map((t) => {
                const q = qtys[t.code] || 0;
                return (
                  <View
                    key={t.code}
                    style={{
                      backgroundColor: '#fff',
                      borderWidth: 1,
                      borderColor: '#eee',
                      borderRadius: 10,
                      padding: 12,
                      flexDirection: 'row',
                      justifyContent: 'space-between',
                      alignItems: 'center',
                      gap: 12,
                    }}
                  >
                    <View style={{ flex: 1, paddingRight: 8 }}>
                      <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontWeight: '600' }}>
                        {t.name}
                      </Text>
                      <Text style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: 12 }}>
                        {formatTime(t.time_reward)} Â· {formatMoney(t.money_reward_eur)}
                      </Text>
                    </View>

                    {/* Qty controls */}
                    <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                      <Pressable
                        onPress={() => dec(t.code)}
                        style={{
                          width: 36,
                          height: 36,
                          borderRadius: 10,
                          borderWidth: 1,
                          borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
                          backgroundColor: '#f8fafc',
                          alignItems: 'center',
                          justifyContent: 'center',
                        }}
                      >
                        <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontSize: 18 }}>âˆ’</Text>
                      </Pressable>

                      <TextInput
                        value={String(q)}
                        onChangeText={(txt) => onEdit(t.code, txt)}
                        keyboardType="number-pad"
                        inputMode="numeric"
                        maxLength={3}
                        style={{
                          width: 56,
                          height: 36,
                          textAlign: 'center',
                          color: '#111',
                          backgroundColor: '#fff',
                          borderWidth: 1,
                          borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
                          borderRadius: 8,
                          paddingVertical: 6,
                        }}
                      />

                      <Pressable
                        onPress={() => inc(t.code)}
                        style={{
                          width: 36,
                          height: 36,
                          borderRadius: 10,
                          borderWidth: 1,
                          borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
                          backgroundColor: '#f8fafc',
                          alignItems: 'center',
                          justifyContent: 'center',
                        }}
                      >
                        <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontSize: 18 }}>ï¼‹</Text>
                      </Pressable>
                    </View>
                  </View>
                );
              })}
            </View>
          ))}

        {/* Footer summary (submit arrives in Step 4) */}
        {!loading && !error && (
          <View
            style={{
              marginTop: 8,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
              borderWidth: 1,
              borderColor: '#eee',
              backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
              flexDirection: 'row',
              justifyContent: 'space-between',
              alignItems: 'center',
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#333' }}>
              Selected items: <Text style={{ fontWeight: '700' }}>{totalSelected}</Text>
            </Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#999' }}>
              Submit button arrives in Step 4
            </Text>
          </View>
        )}
      </ScrollView>
    </SafeAreaView>
  );
}

// Temporary hard-coded IDs for Phase 2.

src/api/submissions.ts (new)
// src/api/submissions.ts
import { apiFetch } from './client';

export type SubmissionItem = { task_code: string; quantity: number };

export type SubmissionResponse = {
  submission_id: string | null;
  total_time_minutes: number | string;
  total_money_eur: number | string;
  // Optional diagnostics from our n8n query (may not always be present)
  user_error?: number;
  missing_task_count?: number;
};

export async function submitSubmission(payload: {
  adult_id: string;
  child_id: string;
  items: SubmissionItem[];
}) {
  return apiFetch<SubmissionResponse>('/api/submissions', {
    method: 'POST',
    body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  });
}
app/(tabs)/form.tsx (replace with this)
// app/(tabs)/form.tsx
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import {
  ActivityIndicator,
  SafeAreaView,
  ScrollView,
  Text,
  View,
  Pressable,
  TextInput,
} from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { getTasks, Task, TimeReward } from '../../src/api/tasks';
import { submitSubmission } from '../../src/api/submissions';
import { ADULT_ID, CHILD_ID } from '../../src/config';

function formatTime(t: TimeReward) {
  switch (t) {
    case 'MIN_15': return '15 min';
    case 'HOUR_1': return '1 hour';
    case 'NEG_MIN_15': return 'âˆ’15 min';
    case 'NEG_HOUR_1': return 'âˆ’1 hour';
    default: return 'â€“';
  }
}
function formatMoney(v: string | number) {
  const n = Number(v || 0);
  const sign = n < 0 ? '-' : '';
  return `${sign}â‚¬${Math.abs(n).toFixed(2)}`;
}

type QtyMap = Record<string, number>;

export default function FormScreen() {
  const router = useRouter();

  // Load state
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<Task[]>([]);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Local qty state
  const [qtys, setQtys] = useState<QtyMap>({});

  // Submit state
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [submitErr, setSubmitErr] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [submitOk, setSubmitOk] = useState<{ time: string; money: string } | null>(null);

  // Load tasks on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    (async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true);
        setError(null);
        const data = await getTasks();
        const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
        if (!cancelled) {
          setTasks(arr);
          setQtys((prev) => {
            const next = { ...prev };
            for (const t of arr) if (next[t.code] == null) next[t.code] = 0;
            return next;
          });
        }
      } catch (e: any) {
        if (!cancelled) setError(e?.message || 'Failed to load tasks');
      } finally {
        if (!cancelled) setLoading(false);
      }
    })();
    return () => { cancelled = true; };
  }, []);

  // Group by category
  const groups = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<string, Task[]>();
    for (const t of tasks) {
      const k = t.category || 'Other';
      if (!map.has(k)) map.set(k, []);
      map.get(k)!.push(t);
    }
    const arr = Array.from(map.entries()).map(([category, items]) => ({
      category,
      items: items.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name)),
    }));
    return arr.sort((a, b) => a.category.localeCompare(b.category));
  }, [tasks]);

  // Qty helpers
  const clamp = (n: number) => Math.max(0, Math.min(999, Number.isFinite(n) ? Math.trunc(n) : 0));
  const setQty = (code: string, value: number) =>
    setQtys((prev) => ({ ...prev, [code]: clamp(value) }));
  const inc = (code: string) => setQty(code, (qtys[code] || 0) + 1);
  const dec = (code: string) => setQty(code, (qtys[code] || 0) - 1);
  const onEdit = (code: string, text: string) => {
    const digitsOnly = text.replace(/[^\d]/g, '');
    setQty(code, digitsOnly === '' ? 0 : parseInt(digitsOnly, 10));
  };

  const totalSelected = useMemo(
    () => Object.values(qtys).reduce((a, b) => a + (Number.isFinite(b) ? b : 0), 0),
    [qtys]
  );

  // Build items for submission
  const itemsToSubmit = useMemo(
    () =>
      Object.entries(qtys)
        .filter(([, q]) => (q || 0) > 0)
        .map(([task_code, quantity]) => ({ task_code, quantity })),
    [qtys]
  );

  async function onSubmit() {
    if (submitting || itemsToSubmit.length === 0) return;
    try {
      setSubmitting(true);
      setSubmitErr(null);
      setSubmitOk(null);

      const res = await submitSubmission({
        adult_id: ADULT_ID,
        child_id: CHILD_ID,
        items: itemsToSubmit,
      });

      // Normalize totals to strings for display
      const t = String((res as any)?.total_time_minutes ?? '0');
      const m = String((res as any)?.total_money_eur ?? '0');

      setSubmitOk({ time: t, money: m });
      // Clear selections
      setQtys((prev) => {
        const next: QtyMap = { ...prev };
        for (const k of Object.keys(next)) next[k] = 0;
        return next;
      });
    } catch (e: any) {
      setSubmitErr(e?.message || 'Failed to submit');
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }}>
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={{ padding: 24, gap: 16 }} keyboardShouldPersistTaps="handled">
        <Text style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: '700', color: '#111' }}>Form</Text>

        {/* Submitting banners */}
        {submitOk && (
          <View style={{ backgroundColor: '#e8f7ee', borderColor: '#b9e4c6', borderWidth: 1, padding: 12, borderRadius: 10, gap: 6 }}>
            <Text style={{ color: '#127c39', fontWeight: '700' }}>Submitted âœ“</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#127c39' }}>
              Time: {submitOk.time} â€¢ Money: â‚¬{Number(submitOk.money).toFixed ? Number(submitOk.money).toFixed(2) : submitOk.money}
            </Text>
            <Pressable onPress={() => router.replace('/(tabs)/totals')} style={{ paddingVertical: 8 }}>
              <Text style={{ color: '#2d6cdf' }}>Go to Totals</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
        )}
        {submitErr && (
          <View style={{ backgroundColor: '#fde7e9', borderColor: '#f2b2b8', borderWidth: 1, padding: 12, borderRadius: 10 }}>
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{submitErr}</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Loading */}
        {loading && (
          <View style={{ paddingVertical: 32, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            <ActivityIndicator />
            <Text style={{ marginTop: 8, color: '#666' }}>Loading tasksâ€¦</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Error */}
        {!loading && error && (
          <View style={{ backgroundColor: '#fde7e9', borderColor: '#f2b2b8', borderWidth: 1, padding: 12, borderRadius: 10 }}>
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{error}</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Empty */}
        {!loading && !error && groups.length === 0 && (
          <View style={{ backgroundColor: '#fafafa', borderColor: '#eee', borderWidth: 1, padding: 16, borderRadius: 10 }}>
            <Text style={{ color: '#333', fontWeight: '600' }}>No tasks</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>There are no active tasks right now.</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* List with quantity controls */}
        {!loading && !error && groups.map(({ category, items }) => (
          <View key={category} style={{ backgroundColor: '#fafafa', borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#eee', borderRadius: 12, padding: 12, gap: 8 }}>
            <Text style={{ color: '#222', fontWeight: '700' }}>{category}</Text>

            {items.map((t) => {
              const q = qtys[t.code] || 0;
              return (
                <View
                  key={t.code}
                  style={{
                    backgroundColor: '#fff',
                    borderWidth: 1,
                    borderColor: '#eee',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    padding: 12,
                    flexDirection: 'row',
                    justifyContent: 'space-between',
                    alignItems: 'center',
                    gap: 12,
                  }}
                >
                  <View style={{ flex: 1, paddingRight: 8 }}>
                    <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontWeight: '600' }}>{t.name}</Text>
                    <Text style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: 12 }}>
                      {formatTime(t.time_reward)} Â· {formatMoney(t.money_reward_eur)}
                    </Text>
                  </View>

                  {/* Qty controls */}
                  <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                    <Pressable
                      onPress={() => dec(t.code)}
                      style={{
                        width: 36,
                        height: 36,
                        borderRadius: 10,
                        borderWidth: 1,
                        borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
                        backgroundColor: '#f8fafc',
                        alignItems: 'center',
                        justifyContent: 'center',
                      }}
                    >
                      <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontSize: 18 }}>âˆ’</Text>
                    </Pressable>

                    <TextInput
                      value={String(q)}
                      onChangeText={(txt) => onEdit(t.code, txt)}
                      keyboardType="number-pad"
                      inputMode="numeric"
                      maxLength={3}
                      style={{
                        width: 56,
                        height: 36,
                        textAlign: 'center',
                        color: '#111',
                        backgroundColor: '#fff',
                        borderWidth: 1,
                        borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
                        borderRadius: 8,
                        paddingVertical: 6,
                      }}
                    />

                    <Pressable
                      onPress={() => inc(t.code)}
                      style={{
                        width: 36,
                        height: 36,
                        borderRadius: 10,
                        borderWidth: 1,
                        borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
                        backgroundColor: '#f8fafc',
                        alignItems: 'center',
                        justifyContent: 'center',
                      }}
                    >
                      <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontSize: 18 }}>ï¼‹</Text>

              );
            })}
          </View>
        ))}

        {/* Footer with Submit */}
        {!loading && !error && (
          <View style={{ marginTop: 8, gap: 10 }}>
            <Pressable
              onPress={onSubmit}
              disabled={submitting || itemsToSubmit.length === 0}
              style={{
                opacity: submitting || itemsToSubmit.length === 0 ? 0.5 : 1,

                paddingVertical: 14,

            >
              <Text style={{ color: '#fff', fontWeight: '700' }}>
                {submitting ? 'Submittingâ€¦' : `Submit (${itemsToSubmit.length} items)`}
              </Text>

          </View>
        )}
      </ScrollView>
    </SafeAreaView>

}

Option C â€” Supabase SQL (direct DB check)

SELECT
  t.code,
  t.name,
  t.category,
  SUM(si.time_minutes_awarded)  AS time_minutes_total,
  SUM(si.money_awarded_eur)     AS money_total_eur
FROM submission_item si
JOIN submission s ON s.id = si.submission_id
JOIN task t       ON t.id = si.task_id
WHERE s.child_id = '0dc586a8-a7ae-48fb-874b-1aab47a0cdb0'
  AND si.payout_id IS NULL
GROUP BY t.code, t.name, t.category
ORDER BY t.category, t.name;

403 â†’ you added role gates on backend (submissions.create) and the current user isnâ€™t allowed.

â€œNetwork request failedâ€ â†’ check your API_BASE and that n8n flows are Activated (production /webhook/...).

Thought for 39s
Perfect â€” Phase 3 / Step 1â€“4 for Totals & Toggles.

1) src/api/totals.ts
// src/api/totals.ts
import { apiFetch } from './client';

export type TotalsRow = {
  code: string;
  name: string;
  category: string;
  time_minutes_total: number | string; // n8n may return strings
  money_total_eur: number | string;
};

export async function getTotals(childId: string) {
  return apiFetch<TotalsRow[]>(
    `/api/totals?child_id=${encodeURIComponent(childId)}`,
    { method: 'GET' },
  );
}
2) src/api/preferences.ts
// src/api/preferences.ts
import { apiFetch } from './client';

export type Preference = 'TIME' | 'MONEY';

export async function setPreference(payload: {
  child_id: string;
  task_code: string;
  preference: Preference;
}) {
  return apiFetch('/api/preferences', {
    method: 'POST',
    body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  });
}
3) app/(tabs)/totals.tsx (replace file)
// app/(tabs)/totals.tsx
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import {
  ActivityIndicator,
  RefreshControl,
  SafeAreaView,
  ScrollView,
  Text,
  View,
  Pressable,
} from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { getTotals, TotalsRow } from '../../src/api/totals';
import { setPreference, Preference } from '../../src/api/preferences';
import { CHILD_ID } from '../../src/config';
import { useAuth } from '../../src/state/auth';

function toNumber(v: number | string | null | undefined) {
  const n = Number(v ?? 0);
  return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : 0;
}

export default function TotalsScreen() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user, ready, signOut } = useAuth();
  const isAdmin = user?.role === 'admin';

  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [refreshing, setRefreshing] = useState(false);
  const [rows, setRows] = useState<TotalsRow[]>([]);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Local preference state (optimistic UI). Default to MONEY when both present.
  const [prefs, setPrefs] = useState<Record<string, Preference>>({});

  async function fetchTotals(initial = false) {
    try {
      if (initial) setLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      const data = await getTotals(CHILD_ID);
      const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
      setRows(arr);

      // Initialize default preferences (only for rows that can choose)
      setPrefs((prev) => {
        const next = { ...prev };
        for (const r of arr) {
          const time = toNumber(r.time_minutes_total);
          const money = toNumber(r.money_total_eur);
          const code = r.code;
          const canChoose = time > 0 && Math.abs(money) > 0;
          if (canChoose && !next[code]) next[code] = 'MONEY'; // default like backend
        }
        return next;
      });
    } catch (e: any) {
      const msg = e?.message || 'Failed to load totals';
      // Auto-logout on unauthorized
      if (msg === 'unauthorized') {
        await signOut();
        router.replace('/');
        return;
      }
      setError(msg);
    } finally {
      if (initial) setLoading(false);
      setRefreshing(false);
    }
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchTotals(true);
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, []);

  // Group by category for display
  const groups = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<string, TotalsRow[]>();
    for (const r of rows) {
      const k = r.category || 'Other';
      if (!map.has(k)) map.set(k, []);
      map.get(k)!.push(r);
    }
    // Sort categories and rows by name for a stable UI
    return Array.from(map.entries())
      .map(([category, items]) => ({
        category,
        items: items.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name)),
      }))
      .sort((a, b) => a.category.localeCompare(b.category));
  }, [rows]);

  async function onToggle(code: string, pref: Preference) {
    // Find the row; allow toggle only when both time & money exist
    const row = rows.find((r) => r.code === code);
    if (!row) return;
    const time = toNumber(row.time_minutes_total);
    const money = toNumber(row.money_total_eur);
    const canChoose = time > 0 && Math.abs(money) > 0;
    if (!canChoose) return;

    // Optimistic update
    const prev = prefs[code];
    setPrefs((p) => ({ ...p, [code]: pref }));

    try {
      await setPreference({ child_id: CHILD_ID, task_code: code, preference: pref });
    } catch (e) {
      // Rollback on error
      setPrefs((p) => ({ ...p, [code]: prev }));
    }
  }

  const totalTasksPending = rows.length;

  return (
    <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }}>
      <ScrollView
        contentContainerStyle={{ padding: 24, gap: 16 }}
        refreshControl={
          <RefreshControl
            refreshing={refreshing}
            onRefresh={() => {
              setRefreshing(true);
              fetchTotals(false);
            }}
            tintColor="#2d6cdf"
          />
        }
      >
        {/* Header */}
        <View style={{ gap: 4 }}>
          <Text style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: '700', color: '#111' }}>Totals</Text>
          {loading ? null : (
            <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>
              {totalTasksPending > 0
                ? `${totalTasksPending} task${totalTasksPending > 1 ? 's' : ''} pending`
                : 'Nothing pending'}
            </Text>
          )}
        </View>

        {/* Admin shortcut to Payout tab (optional) */}
        {isAdmin && (
          <Pressable
            onPress={() => router.replace('/(tabs)/payout')}
            style={{
              alignSelf: 'flex-start',
              backgroundColor: '#eef2ff',
              borderColor: '#c7d2fe',
              borderWidth: 1,
              paddingVertical: 8,
              paddingHorizontal: 12,
              borderRadius: 8,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#4338ca', fontWeight: '600' }}>Go to Payout</Text>
          </Pressable>
        )}

        {/* Loading */}
        {loading && (
          <View style={{ paddingVertical: 32, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            <ActivityIndicator />
            <Text style={{ marginTop: 8, color: '#666' }}>Loading totalsâ€¦</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Error */}
        {!loading && error && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fde7e9',
              borderColor: '#f2b2b8',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{error}</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Empty */}
        {!loading && !error && groups.length === 0 && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
              borderColor: '#eee',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 16,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#333', fontWeight: '600' }}>No pending items</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>
              Submit items from the Form tab, then refresh this page.
            </Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* List */}
        {!loading &&
          !error &&
          groups.map(({ category, items }) => (
            <View
              key={category}
              style={{
                backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
                borderWidth: 1,
                borderColor: '#eee',
                borderRadius: 12,
                padding: 12,
                gap: 8,
              }}
            >
              <Text style={{ color: '#222', fontWeight: '700' }}>{category}</Text>

              {items.map((r) => {
                const time = toNumber(r.time_minutes_total);
                const money = toNumber(r.money_total_eur);
                const canChoose = time > 0 && Math.abs(money) > 0;

                const currentPref = prefs[r.code] ?? (canChoose ? 'MONEY' : undefined);

                return (
                  <View
                    key={r.code}
                    style={{
                      backgroundColor: '#fff',
                      borderWidth: 1,
                      borderColor: '#eee',
                      borderRadius: 10,
                      padding: 12,
                      gap: 6,
                    }}
                  >
                    <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontWeight: '600' }}>{r.name}</Text>
                    <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', gap: 12 }}>
                      <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>Time: {time} min</Text>
                      <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>Money: â‚¬{toNumber(money).toFixed(2)}</Text>
                    </View>

                    {/* Toggle or Fixed */}
                    {canChoose ? (
                      <View
                        style={{
                          flexDirection: 'row',
                          gap: 8,
                          alignItems: 'center',
                        }}
                      >
                        <Segmented
                          value={currentPref as Preference}
                          onChange={(v) => onToggle(r.code, v)}
                        />
                        <Text style={{ color: '#999', fontSize: 12 }}>
                          Preference applies at payout
                        </Text>
                      </View>
                    ) : (
                      <Text style={{ color: '#999', fontSize: 12 }}>
                        Fixed: {time > 0 ? 'Time' : 'Money'}
                      </Text>
                    )}
                  </View>
                );
              })}
            </View>
          ))}
      </ScrollView>
    </SafeAreaView>
  );
}

/** Simple segmented control for TIME / MONEY */
function Segmented({
  value,
  onChange,
}: {
  value: Preference;
  onChange: (v: Preference) => void;
}) {
  const isTime = value === 'TIME';
  return (
    <View
      style={{
        borderWidth: 1,
        borderColor: '#e5e7eb',
        borderRadius: 999,
        overflow: 'hidden',
        flexDirection: 'row',
      }}
    >
      <Pressable
        onPress={() => onChange('TIME')}
        style={{
          paddingVertical: 6,
          paddingHorizontal: 12,
          backgroundColor: isTime ? '#2d6cdf' : '#fff',
        }}
      >
        <Text style={{ color: isTime ? '#fff' : '#111' }}>Time</Text>
      </Pressable>
      <Pressable
        onPress={() => onChange('MONEY')}
        style={{
          paddingVertical: 6,
          paddingHorizontal: 12,
          backgroundColor: !isTime ? '#2d6cdf' : '#fff',
        }}
      >
        <Text style={{ color: !isTime ? '#fff' : '#111' }}>Money</Text>
      </Pressable>
    </View>
  );
}
What you can do now

For fixed rows (only time or only money), the UI shows Fixed: â€¦.

If you want, next we can add a tiny toast on success/failure, or move on to Phase 4: Payout (Admin).

1) src/api/payout.ts (new file)
// src/api/payout.ts
import { apiFetch } from './client';

export type PreviewLine = {
  code: string;
  name: string;
  category: string;
  chosen_time: number | string;
  chosen_money: number | string;
};

export type PreviewResponse = {
  lines: PreviewLine[] | null;
  total_time_minutes: number | string;
  total_money_eur: number | string;
};

// The n8n respond node can send an object or an array with a single object.
// This normalizer makes the UI tolerant to both.
function normalizePreview(raw: any): PreviewResponse {
  const data = Array.isArray(raw) ? raw[0] : raw;
  const lines = (data?.lines ?? null) as PreviewLine[] | null;
  return {
    lines,
    total_time_minutes: data?.total_time_minutes ?? 0,
    total_money_eur: data?.total_money_eur ?? 0,
  };
}

export async function getPayoutPreview(childId: string) {
  const raw = await apiFetch<PreviewResponse | PreviewResponse[]>(
    `/api/payout/preview?child_id=${encodeURIComponent(childId)}`,
    { method: 'GET' }
  );
  return normalizePreview(raw);
}

export type ConfirmResponse = {
  payout_id: string | null;
  total_time_minutes: number | string;
  total_money_eur: number | string;
  lines_inserted?: number | string;
  items_marked_paid?: number | string;
  did_payout?: 0 | 1;
};

export async function confirmPayout(payload: {
  child_id: string;
  approved_by_admin_id: string;
}) {
  return apiFetch<ConfirmResponse>('/api/payout/confirm', {
    method: 'POST',
    body: JSON.stringify(payload),
  });
}
2) app/(tabs)/payout.tsx (replace file)
// app/(tabs)/payout.tsx
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import {
  ActivityIndicator,
  RefreshControl,
  SafeAreaView,
  ScrollView,
  Text,
  View,
  Pressable,
} from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { useAuth } from '../../src/state/auth';
import { CHILD_ID } from '../../src/config';
import { getPayoutPreview, confirmPayout, PreviewLine } from '../../src/api/payout';

function n(v: number | string | null | undefined) {
  const x = Number(v ?? 0);
  return Number.isFinite(x) ? x : 0;
}

export default function PayoutScreen() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user, ready, signOut } = useAuth();
  const isAdmin = user?.role === 'admin';

  // Admin-only guard (front-end UX);
  // backend also enforces admin, so this is just nicer messaging.
  if (ready && !isAdmin) {
    return (
      <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }}>
        <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={{ padding: 24, gap: 16 }}>
          <Text style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: '700', color: '#111' }}>Payout</Text>
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fff7ed',
              borderColor: '#fed7aa',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
              gap: 6,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#9a3412' }}>Admin only</Text>
            <Pressable onPress={() => router.replace('/(tabs)/totals')}>
              <Text style={{ color: '#2d6cdf' }}>Go to Totals</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
        </ScrollView>
      </SafeAreaView>
    );
  }

  // Screen state
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [refreshing, setRefreshing] = useState(false);
  const [lines, setLines] = useState<PreviewLine[] | null>(null);
  const [totalTime, setTotalTime] = useState<number>(0);
  const [totalMoney, setTotalMoney] = useState<number>(0);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Confirm state
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [ok, setOk] = useState<{ payout_id: string; time: number; money: number } | null>(null);
  const [submitErr, setSubmitErr] = useState<string | null>(null);

  async function fetchPreview(initial = false) {
    try {
      if (initial) setLoading(true);
      setError(null);
      const data = await getPayoutPreview(CHILD_ID);
      setLines(data.lines ?? []);
      setTotalTime(n(data.total_time_minutes));
      setTotalMoney(n(data.total_money_eur));
    } catch (e: any) {
      const msg = e?.message || 'Failed to load payout preview';
      if (msg === 'unauthorized') {
        await signOut();
        router.replace('/');
        return;
      }
      if (msg === 'forbidden') {
        setError('Forbidden (admin only)');
      } else {
        setError(msg);
      }
    } finally {
      if (initial) setLoading(false);
      setRefreshing(false);
    }
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isAdmin) fetchPreview(true);
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [isAdmin]);

  const hasAnythingToPay = useMemo(
    () => totalTime > 0 || Math.abs(totalMoney) > 0,
    [totalTime, totalMoney]
  );

  async function onConfirm() {
    if (!isAdmin || submitting || !hasAnythingToPay) return;
    try {
      setSubmitting(true);
      setSubmitErr(null);
      setOk(null);
      const resp = await confirmPayout({
        child_id: CHILD_ID,
        approved_by_admin_id: user!.user_id,
      });
      const time = n(resp.total_time_minutes);
      const money = n(resp.total_money_eur);
      setOk({ payout_id: String(resp.payout_id || ''), time, money });
      // Refresh preview (should be empty now)
      await fetchPreview(false);
    } catch (e: any) {
      const msg = e?.message || 'Failed to confirm payout';
      if (msg === 'unauthorized') {
        await signOut();
        router.replace('/');
        return;
      }
      if (msg === 'forbidden') {
        setSubmitErr('Forbidden (admin only)');
      } else {
        setSubmitErr(msg);
      }
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }}>
      <ScrollView
        contentContainerStyle={{ padding: 24, gap: 16 }}
        refreshControl={
          <RefreshControl
            refreshing={refreshing}
            onRefresh={() => {
              setRefreshing(true);
              fetchPreview(false);
            }}
            tintColor="#2d6cdf"
          />
        }
      >
        {/* Header */}
        <View style={{ gap: 4 }}>
          <Text style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: '700', color: '#111' }}>Payout (Admin)</Text>
          {!loading && (
            <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>
              Time: {totalTime} min â€¢ Money: â‚¬{totalMoney.toFixed(2)}
            </Text>
          )}
        </View>

        {/* Success banner */}
        {ok && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#e8f7ee',
              borderColor: '#b9e4c6',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
              gap: 6,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#127c39', fontWeight: '700' }}>Payout confirmed âœ“</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#127c39' }}>
              ID: {ok.payout_id || '(n/a)'} â€” Time: {ok.time} min â€¢ Money: â‚¬{ok.money.toFixed(2)}
            </Text>
            <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', gap: 16 }}>
              <Pressable onPress={() => router.replace('/(tabs)/history')}>
                <Text style={{ color: '#2d6cdf' }}>Go to History</Text>
              </Pressable>
              <Pressable onPress={() => router.replace('/(tabs)/totals')}>
                <Text style={{ color: '#2d6cdf' }}>Go to Totals</Text>
              </Pressable>
            </View>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Error banners */}
        {error && !loading && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fde7e9',
              borderColor: '#f2b2b8',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{error}</Text>
          </View>
        )}
        {submitErr && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fde7e9',
              borderColor: '#f2b2b8',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 12,
              borderRadius: 10,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{submitErr}</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Loading */}
        {loading && (
          <View style={{ paddingVertical: 32, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            <ActivityIndicator />
            <Text style={{ marginTop: 8, color: '#666' }}>Loading payout previewâ€¦</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Empty */}
        {!loading && !error && !hasAnythingToPay && (
          <View
            style={{
              backgroundColor: '#fafafa',
              borderColor: '#eee',
              borderWidth: 1,
              padding: 16,
              borderRadius: 10,
              gap: 6,
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#333', fontWeight: '600' }}>Nothing to pay</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>
              Add items in Form or adjust preferences in Totals, then refresh.
            </Text>
            <Pressable onPress={() => router.replace('/(tabs)/totals')} style={{ paddingTop: 4 }}>
              <Text style={{ color: '#2d6cdf' }}>Go to Totals</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Preview list */}
        {!loading && !error && hasAnythingToPay && Array.isArray(lines) && lines.length > 0 && (
          <View style={{ gap: 12 }}>
            {lines
              .slice()
              .sort((a, b) => a.category.localeCompare(b.category) || a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
              .map((l) => (
                <View
                  key={l.code}
                  style={{
                    backgroundColor: '#fff',
                    borderWidth: 1,
                    borderColor: '#eee',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    padding: 12,
                    gap: 4,
                  }}
                >
                  <Text style={{ color: '#111', fontWeight: '600' }}>{l.name}</Text>
                  <Text style={{ color: '#666', fontSize: 12 }}>{l.category}</Text>
                  <View style={{ flexDirection: 'row', gap: 12 }}>
                    <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>Time: {n(l.chosen_time)} min</Text>
                    <Text style={{ color: '#666' }}>Money: â‚¬{n(l.chosen_money).toFixed(2)}</Text>
                  </View>
                </View>
              ))}
          </View>
        )}

        {/* Confirm button */}
        {!loading && !error && (
          <Pressable
            onPress={onConfirm}
            disabled={!hasAnythingToPay || submitting}
            style={{
              marginTop: 12,
              opacity: !hasAnythingToPay || submitting ? 0.5 : 1,
              backgroundColor: '#2d6cdf',
              paddingVertical: 14,
              borderRadius: 10,
              alignItems: 'center',
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#fff', fontWeight: '700' }}>
              {submitting ? 'Confirmingâ€¦' : 'Confirm Payout'}
            </Text>
          </Pressable>
        )}
      </ScrollView>
    </SafeAreaView>
  );
}

Short, honest answer: itâ€™s not normal for those screens to be â€œjust UIâ€. Theyâ€™re already wired to your n8n backend. If nothing changes when you tap Submit or flip Time/Money, it means one of these is off:

the n8n workflows arenâ€™t Activated (so /webhook/... returns nothing),

the app isnâ€™t sending or the backend isnâ€™t accepting your token,

the IDs weâ€™re using (adult/child) donâ€™t match DB expectations.

Hereâ€™s how to verify fast, and one small improvement so you arenâ€™t blocked by a hard-coded adult ID.

3-minute verification (web DevTools â†’ Network)
With the app open, go to the Totals or Form tab and:

Form loads tasks â†’ you should see a GET to /api/tasks with 200.

Tap + on a task, then Submit â†’ you should see a POST to /api/submissions with 200.

If itâ€™s 401/403, the token or role gate is the issue (we can fixâ€”see next).

On 200 the green banner should appear, and the quantities reset to 0.

Go to Totals â†’ you should see a GET /api/totals?child_id=â€¦ with 200 and the pending numbers.

Flip a toggle â†’ a POST /api/preferences with 200.

Payout (admin) â†’ GET /api/payout/preview?child_id=â€¦ with 200; Confirm sends POST /api/payout/confirm.

If any of those calls donâ€™t appear or arenâ€™t 200, tell me the status code you seeâ€”weâ€™ll target just that step.

Likely culprit & quick fix: adult ID
Right now the Form screen uses a hard-coded ADULT_ID from src/config.ts. If youâ€™re logged in as a different adult (or you switch users), that can silently cause backend checks to fail. Letâ€™s use the actual logged-in user ID instead.

Replace app/(tabs)/form.tsx with this version (only change: use logged-in user.user_id)
// app/(tabs)/form.tsx
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import {
  ActivityIndicator,
  SafeAreaView,
  ScrollView,
  Text,
  View,
  Pressable,
  TextInput,
} from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { getTasks, Task, TimeReward } from '../../src/api/tasks';
import { submitSubmission } from '../../src/api/submissions';
import { CHILD_ID } from '../../src/config';            // keep child for now
import { useAuth } from '../../src/state/auth';         // <-- use logged-in user

function formatTime(t: TimeReward) {
  switch (t) {
    case 'MIN_15': return '15 min';
    case 'HOUR_1': return '1 hour';
    case 'NEG_MIN_15': return 'âˆ’15 min';
    case 'NEG_HOUR_1': return 'âˆ’1 hour';
    default: return 'â€“';
  }
}
function formatMoney(v: string | number) {
  const n = Number(v || 0);
  const sign = n < 0 ? '-' : '';
  return `${sign}â‚¬${Math.abs(n).toFixed(2)}`;
}

type QtyMap = Record<string, number>;

export default function FormScreen() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user } = useAuth();                           // <-- here
  const ADULT_ID = user?.user_id ?? '';                 // <-- use current user id

  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState<Task[]>([]);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const [qtys, setQtys] = useState<QtyMap>({});
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [submitErr, setSubmitErr] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [submitOk, setSubmitOk] = useState<{ time: string; money: string } | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;
    (async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true); setError(null);
        const data = await getTasks();
        const arr = Array.isArray(data) ? data : [];
        if (!cancelled) {
          setTasks(arr);
          setQtys(prev => {
            const next = { ...prev };
            for (const t of arr) if (next[t.code] == null) next[t.code] = 0;
            return next;
          });
        }
      } catch (e: any) {
        if (!cancelled) setError(e?.message || 'Failed to load tasks');
      } finally {
        if (!cancelled) setLoading(false);
      }
    })();
    return () => { cancelled = true; };
  }, []);

  const groups = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map<string, Task[]>();
    for (const t of tasks) {
      const k = t.category || 'Other';
      if (!map.has(k)) map.set(k, []);
      map.get(k)!.push(t);
    }
    return Array.from(map.entries())
      .map(([category, items]) => ({ category, items: items.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name)) }))
      .sort((a, b) => a.category.localeCompare(b.category));
  }, [tasks]);

  const clamp = (n: number) => Math.max(0, Math.min(999, Number.isFinite(n) ? Math.trunc(n) : 0));
  const setQty = (code: string, value: number) => setQtys(prev => ({ ...prev, [code]: clamp(value) }));
  const inc = (code: string) => setQty(code, (qtys[code] || 0) + 1);
  const dec = (code: string) => setQty(code, (qtys[code] || 0) - 1);
  const onEdit = (code: string, text: string) => {
    const digitsOnly = text.replace(/[^\d]/g, '');
    setQty(code, digitsOnly === '' ? 0 : parseInt(digitsOnly, 10));
  };

  const itemsToSubmit = useMemo(
    () => Object.entries(qtys).filter(([, q]) => (q || 0) > 0).map(([task_code, quantity]) => ({ task_code, quantity })),
    [qtys]
  );

  async function onSubmit() {
    if (submitting || itemsToSubmit.length === 0) return;
    try {
      setSubmitting(true); setSubmitErr(null); setSubmitOk(null);

      if (!ADULT_ID) throw new Error('No logged-in user');
      const res = await submitSubmission({
        adult_id: ADULT_ID,     // <-- current user
        child_id: CHILD_ID,     // <-- keep hardcoded child for now
        items: itemsToSubmit,
      });

      const t = String((res as any)?.total_time_minutes ?? '0');
      const m = String((res as any)?.total_money_eur ?? '0');
      setSubmitOk({ time: t, money: m });

      setQtys(prev => {
        const next: QtyMap = { ...prev };
        for (const k of Object.keys(next)) next[k] = 0;
        return next;
      });
    } catch (e: any) {
      setSubmitErr(e?.message || 'Failed to submit');
    } finally {
      setSubmitting(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <SafeAreaView style={{ flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#fff' }}>
      <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={{ padding: 24, gap: 16 }} keyboardShouldPersistTaps="handled">
        <Text style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: '700', color: '#111' }}>Form</Text>

        {submitOk && (
          <View style={{ backgroundColor: '#e8f7ee', borderColor: '#b9e4c6', borderWidth: 1, padding: 12, borderRadius: 10, gap: 6 }}>
            <Text style={{ color: '#127c39', fontWeight: '700' }}>Submitted âœ“</Text>
            <Text style={{ color: '#127c39' }}>
              Time: {submitOk.time} â€¢ Money: â‚¬{Number(submitOk.money).toFixed ? Number(submitOk.money).toFixed(2) : submitOk.money}
            </Text>
            <Pressable onPress={() => router.replace('/(tabs)/totals')} style={{ paddingVertical: 8 }}>
              <Text style={{ color: '#2d6cdf' }}>Go to Totals</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
        )}
        {submitErr && (
          <View style={{ backgroundColor: '#fde7e9', borderColor: '#f2b2b8', borderWidth: 1, padding: 12, borderRadius: 10 }}>
            <Text style={{ color: '#b00020' }}>{submitErr}</Text>
          </View>
        )}

        {/* loading / error / empty blocks omitted here for brevity â€“ keep what you had from Step 2/3 */}

        {/* â€¦ render groups and qty controls exactly as you have â€¦ */}

        {/* Submit button */}
        <View style={{ marginTop: 8, gap: 10 }}>
          <Pressable
            onPress={onSubmit}
            disabled={submitting || itemsToSubmit.length === 0}
            style={{
              opacity: submitting || itemsToSubmit.length === 0 ? 0.5 : 1,
              backgroundColor: '#2d6cdf',
              paddingVertical: 14,
              borderRadius: 10,
              alignItems: 'center',
            }}
          >
            <Text style={{ color: '#fff', fontWeight: '700' }}>
              {submitting ? 'Submittingâ€¦' : `Submit (${itemsToSubmit.length} items)`}
            </Text>
          </Pressable>
        </View>
      </ScrollView>
    </SafeAreaView>
  );
}
Now the â€œadultâ€ in the payload is whoever is logged in. That removes the biggest source of silent failures.

1) src/state/data.tsx â€” global â€œinvalidateâ€ counter (NEW)
import React, { createContext, useContext, useMemo, useState } from 'react';

/**
 * Very light data-invalidator: whenever you complete a write (submit, preference change, payout),
 * call invalidate(). Any screen that cares can watch `version` and refetch.
 */
type DataCtx = {
  version: number;           // increments on any data change
  invalidate: () => void;    // call this after successful writes
};
const Ctx = createContext<DataCtx | undefined>(undefined);

export function DataProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [version, setVersion] = useState(0);
  const invalidate = () => setVersion((v) => v + 1);
  const value = useMemo(() => ({ version, invalidate }), [version]);
  return <Ctx.Provider value={value}>{children}</Ctx.Provider>;
}

export function useData() {
  const ctx = useContext(Ctx);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error('useData must be used inside <DataProvider>');
  return ctx;
}
